Topic: Math
Question: A computer routine was developed to generate two numbers (x,y) the first being a random number between 0 and 100 inclusive, and the second being less than or equal to the square root of the first. Each of the following pair satisfies the routine except
Choices:
  A: (99,10)
  B: (85,9)
  C: (50,7)
  D: (1,1)
  E: (1,0)
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  - The first number (x) is a random number between 0 and 100 inclusive.
  - The second number (y) is less than or equal to the square root of the first number (x).
  - To check if a pair satisfies the routine, we need to verify that y is less than or equal to the square root of x.
  
Checking each pair:
  - For pair (99,10), 10 is less than or equal to the square root of 99.
  - For pair (85,9), 9 is less than or equal to the square root of 85.
  - For pair (50,7), 7 is less than or equal to the square root of 50.
  - For pair (1,1), 1 is less than or equal to the square root of 1.
  - For pair (1,0), 0 is less than or equal to the square root of 1.

Action: Answer("None of the Above")  
None of the pairs fail to satisfy the routine.

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 2 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: If 75 percent of the employees of a certain company take a winter vacation, 40 percent take a winter and a summer vacation, and 20 percent take neither a winter nor a summer vacation, what Q percent of the employees take a summer vacation but not a winter vacation?
Choices:
  A: 5%
  B: 15%
  C: 25%
  D: 35%
  E: 45%
Response 0:
Let's assume that there are 100 employees in the company. 

Knowledge:
- 75% of the employees take a winter vacation, which means 75 employees take a winter vacation.
- 40% of the employees take a winter and a summer vacation, which means 40 employees take both vacations.
- 20% of the employees take neither a winter nor a summer vacation, which means 20 employees take neither vacation.
- We want to find the percentage of employees who take a summer vacation but not a winter vacation.

To find the percentage of employees who take a summer vacation but not a winter vacation, we need to subtract the number of employees who take both vacations from the number of employees who take only a summer vacation.

The number of employees who take only a summer vacation can be found by subtracting the number of employees who take both vacations from the number of employees who take a summer vacation:
Summer vacation only = Total summer vacation - Both vacations
Summer vacation only = (100-Q)% - 40%

We know that 20% of the employees take neither vacation, so the percentage of employees who take at least one vacation is:
100% - 20% = 80%

We also know that 75% of the employees take a winter vacation, and 40% take both vacations. This means that the percentage of employees who take a summer vacation is:
80% - 75% + 40% = 45%

Now we can substitute the value of the percentage of employees who take a summer vacation into the equation for Summer vacation only:
Summer vacation only = (100-Q)% - 40%
Summer vacation only = 45% - 40%
Summer vacation only = 5%

Action: Answer("A")

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 3 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A rectangular solid, 3 x 4 x 15, is inscribed in a sphere, so that all eight of its vertices are on the sphere. What is the diameter of the sphere?
Choices:
  A:  13.3542
  B:  15.8113
  C:  18.3451
  D:  19.5667
  E:  20.8888
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  A rectangular solid has 8 vertices.
  The diameter of a sphere is twice the radius of the sphere.
  The radius of the sphere is the distance from the center of the sphere to any point on the sphere.
  The longest diagonal of the rectangular solid is the diameter of the sphere.
  The longest diagonal of a rectangular solid can be found using the Pythagorean theorem.
  The Pythagorean theorem states that for a right triangle with legs of length a and b and hypotenuse of length c, a^2 + b^2 = c^2.
  The longest diagonal of the rectangular solid can be found by applying the Pythagorean theorem twice.
  The longest diagonal of the rectangular solid is sqrt(3^2 + 4^2 + 15^2) = sqrt(250).
  The diameter of the sphere is twice the radius of the sphere, which is equal to half the length of the longest diagonal of the rectangular solid.
  Therefore, the diameter of the sphere is 2 * sqrt(250) / 2 = sqrt(250).
Action: Answer("B")

  The longest diagonal of the rectangular solid is sqrt(3^2 + 4^2 + 15^2) = sqrt(250).
  The diameter of the sphere is twice the radius of the sphere, which is equal to half the length of the longest diagonal of the rectangular solid.
  Therefore, the diameter of the sphere is 2 * sqrt(250) / 2 = sqrt(250).
Action: Answer("B")

Question: Peter wants to find 10 additional people to form a scavenger hunt team with him. If he has 10 friends who would like to participate, how many choices does he have for forming his team?
Choices:
  A: 0
  B: 1
  C: 2
  D: 3
  E: 4
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  Peter wants to add 10 people to his team.
  He has 10 friends who would like to participate.
  The order in which the friends are selected does not matter.
  This is a combination problem.
  The formula for combinations is nCr = n! / (r! * (n-r)!), where n is the total number of items, and r is the number of items being chosen.
Action: Answer("C")  
Explanation: 
  Peter has 10 friends to choose from, and he needs to choose 10 of them to join his team. 
  Using the formula for combinations, we get: 
  10C10 = 10! / (10! * (10-10)!) = 10! / (10! * 0!) = 1
  Therefore, Peter has only one choice for forming his team.

Topic: Math
Question: Assistants are needed to prepare for preparation. Each helper can make either 2 large cakes or 35 small cakes/hr. The kitchen is available for 3 hours and 20 large cakes & 700 small cakes are needed. How many helpers are required?
Choices:
  A: 8
  B: 10
  C: 12
  D: 15
  E: 19
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  Each helper can make either 2 large cakes or 35 small cakes/hr.
  The kitchen is available for 3 hours.
  20 large cakes & 700 small cakes are needed.
Calculation:
  Let's calculate how many large cakes and small cakes can be made in 3 hours by one helper:
  - Large cakes: 2 large cakes/hr * 3 hrs = 6 large cakes
  - Small cakes: 35 small cakes/hr * 3 hrs = 105 small cakes
  To make 20 large cakes, we need 20/6 = 3.33 helpers (round up to 4)
  To make 700 small cakes, we need 700/105 = 6.67 helpers (round up to 7)
  Therefore, we need a total of 4 + 7 = 11 helpers.
Action: Answer("B")

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 6 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: An express electric train takes exact three seconds to enter tunnel which is 1 mile long.
If train is traveling at 120 mile an hour, how long will it take to pass completely through the tunnel ?
Choices:
  A: 43 seconds
  B: 39 seconds
  C: 20 seconds
  D: 33 seconds
  E: 55 seconds
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  - The train takes 3 seconds to enter the 1-mile long tunnel, so it will take 3 seconds to exit the tunnel as well.
  - The train's speed is 120 miles per hour.
  - We can use the formula: time = distance / speed
  
Calculation:
  - The train needs to travel 1 mile to pass completely through the tunnel.
  - Using the formula, time = distance / speed = 1 mile / 120 miles per hour = 1/120 hours.
  - We need to convert hours to seconds: 1/120 hours * 3600 seconds/hour = 30 seconds.
  - Adding the time it takes to enter and exit the tunnel, the total time is 3 + 30 + 3 = 36 seconds.

Action: Answer("None of the Above") 
The correct answer is not among the choices. The correct answer is 36 seconds.

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 7 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A bookshelf contains 45 books, 30 of which are hardcover and 20 of which are fiction. What is the maximum number of books that are both hardcover and fiction?
Choices:
  A: 10
  B: 15
  C: 18
  D: 20
  E: 30
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  We can use the formula: Total = Group1 + Group2 - Both + Neither
  We are given:
    Total number of books = 45
    Number of hardcover books = 30
    Number of fiction books = 20
    We want to find the maximum number of books that are both hardcover and fiction.
  We can use the formula to solve for the maximum number of books that are both hardcover and fiction:
    45 = 30 + 20 - Both + Neither
    Simplifying the equation, we get:
    Both - Neither = 5
    Since we want to find the maximum number of books that are both hardcover and fiction, we want to maximize the value of Both.
    The maximum value of Both will occur when the value of Neither is minimized.
    The minimum value of Neither is 0, which means that all 20 fiction books are hardcover.
Action: Answer("B") 
Response 1:
Knowledge:
  We can use the formula: Total = Group1 + Group2 - Both + Neither
  We are given:
    Total number of books = 45
    Number of hardcover books = 30
    Number of fiction books = 20
    We want to find the maximum number of books that are both hardcover and fiction.
  We can use the formula to solve for the maximum number of books that are both hardcover and fiction:
    45 = 30 + 20 - Both + Neither
    Simplifying the equation, we get:
    Both - Neither = 5
    Since we want to find the maximum number of books that are both hardcover and fiction, we want to maximize the value of Both.
    The maximum value of Both will occur when the value of Neither is minimized.
    The minimum value of Neither is 0, which means that all 20 fiction books are hardcover.
Action: Answer("B")

Topic: Math
Question: An electric pole, 14 metres high, casts a shadow of 10 metres. Find the height of a tree that casts a shadow of 15 metres under similar conditions.
Choices:
  A: 21
  B: 22
  C: 20
  D: 23
  E: 24
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  If two objects are similar, then the ratio of their corresponding sides is the same.
  Let h be the height of the tree, and s be the length of its shadow.
  We can set up a proportion: h/s = 14/10
  We can solve for h: h = (14/10) * s

Action: 
  We are given that s = 15.
  h = (14/10) * 15 = 21
  Answer("A")

Topic: Math
Question: At what price should the Karan mark a sewing machine that costs him Rs. 1200/- so that even after offering a 20% discount, he makes 20% profit?
Choices:
  A: 1,879
  B: 1,875
  C: 1,876
  D: 1,872
  E: 1,800
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  Let's assume the marked price of the sewing machine is M.
  The cost price of the sewing machine is Rs. 1200.
  Karan wants to make a 20% profit even after offering a 20% discount.
  Profit = M - 1200
  Selling price after 20% discount = 0.8M
  Karan wants to make a 20% profit on the cost price, so (M - 1200) = 0.2(1200)
  M = 1440 + 1200 = 2640
  The marked price of the sewing machine should be Rs. 2640.
  Selling price after 20% discount = 0.8 * 2640 = 2112
Action: Answer("None of the Above") 
The correct answer is not one of the given choices. The marked price of the sewing machine should be Rs. 2640.

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 10 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: John would make the 3-letter codes with diffenrent 5 vowels and 20 consonants with the condition that the middle letter must be vowel and the first letter and the third letter must be different from each other and are both consonant. How many different codes can be made?
Choices:
  A: 1,980
  B: 2,020
  C: 2,100
  D: 2,200
  E: 1,900
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  There are 5 vowels and 20 consonants.
  The middle letter must be a vowel.
  The first and third letters must be different from each other and both consonants.
  We can choose the first and third letters in 20 * 19 ways.
  We can choose the middle letter in 5 ways.
  We can choose the first and third letters in 18 * 17 ways if we exclude the 2 letters that were chosen for the first and third letters.
  The total number of codes is the product of the number of ways to choose the first and third letters, and the number of ways to choose the middle letter.
  Therefore, the total number of codes is 20 * 19 * 5 * 18 * 17 = 1,938,600.
Action: Answer("A")

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 11 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: At a certain factory, 10 percent of the staplers produced on Monday were defective and 2 percent of the non-defective staplers were rejected by mistake. If 72 of the non-defective staplers were rejected, what was the number of staplers produced that day?
Choices:
  A: 4,000
  B: 4,200
  C: 4,500
  D: 4,800
  E: 5,000
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  Let's assume that the total number of staplers produced on Monday is "x".
  10 percent of the staplers produced on Monday were defective, so the number of defective staplers is 0.1x.
  The remaining staplers are non-defective, so the number of non-defective staplers is 0.9x.
  2 percent of the non-defective staplers were rejected by mistake, so the number of rejected non-defective staplers is 0.02 * 0.9x = 0.018x.
  We know that 72 of the non-defective staplers were rejected, so 0.018x = 72.
  Solving for x, we get x = 4000.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Knowledge:
  Let's assume that the total number of staplers produced on Monday is "x".
  10 percent of the staplers produced on Monday were defective, so the number of defective staplers is 0.1x.
  The remaining staplers are non-defective, so the number of non-defective staplers is 0.9x.
  2 percent of the non-defective staplers were rejected by mistake, so the number of rejected non-defective staplers is 0.02 * 0.9x = 0.018x.
  We know that 72 of the non-defective staplers were rejected, so 0.018x = 72.
  Solving for x, we get x = 4000.

  10 percent of the staplers produced on Monday were defective, so the number of defective staplers is 0.1x.
  The remaining staplers are non-defective, so the number of non-defective staplers is 0.9x.
  2 percent of the non-defective staplers were rejected by mistake, so the number of rejected non-defective staplers is 0.02 * 0.9x = 0.018x.
  We know that 72 of the non-defective staplers were rejected, so 0.018x = 72.
  Solving for x, we get x = 4000.
Action: Answer("A")

Topic: Math
Question: M men agree to purchase a gift for Rs. D. If 3 men drop out how much more will each have to contribute towards the purchase of the gift?
Choices:
  A: D/(M-3)
  B: MD/3
  C: M/(D-3)
  D: 3D/(M2-3M)
  E: None of these
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  Initially, M men agreed to purchase a gift for Rs. D.
  If 3 men drop out, then there will be M-3 men left to purchase the gift.
  Each person's contribution will increase because there are fewer people to share the cost.
  Therefore, the answer should be greater than D/M.

Calculations:
  Initially, each person would contribute D/M.
  After 3 men drop out, each person would have to contribute (D/(M-3)).
  The difference is (D/(M-3)) - (D/M) = 3D/(M^2-3M).
  Therefore, the answer is D: 3D/(M^2-3M).

Action: Answer("D")

Question: Add: +45 and -30
Choices:
  A: -30
  B: +30
  C: 0
  D: 15
  E: -15

  The absolute value of 45 is larger than the absolute value of 30.
  Therefore, +45 and -30 can be added as follows: 45 - 30 = 15.
  The result is positive because the larger number (+45) has a positive sign.

Topic: Math
Question: My wall contains 8 red colour ties, 13 violet colour ties,10 blue colour ties, 5 pink colour ties, 4 green colour ties. If electricity is gone and I want at least two ties of same colour then how many ties I should take out from my rack?
Choices:
  A: 2
  B: 3
  C: 4
  D: 5
  E: 6
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  To ensure that at least two ties are of the same color, we need to apply the Pigeonhole Principle. This principle states that if we have n items to put into m containers, and n > m, then there must be at least one container with more than one item.
  We have 5 different colors of ties, and the total number of ties is 8+13+10+5+4 = 40.
Action: Answer("C")  
Explanation: 
  We need to take out ties until we have at least two ties of the same color. The worst-case scenario is that we take out one tie of each color, which would give us a total of 5 ties. However, if we take out one more tie, we are guaranteed to have at least two ties of the same color. Therefore, we need to take out 4 ties.

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 15 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The events A and B are independent. The probability that event A occurs is 0.6, and the probability that at least one of the events A or B occurs is 0.96. What is the probability that event B occurs?
Choices:
  A: 0.5
  B: 0.6
  C: 0.7
  D: 0.8
  E: 0.9
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  If events A and B are independent, then the probability of both events occurring is the product of their individual probabilities: P(A and B) = P(A) * P(B).
  The probability of at least one of two events occurring is the sum of their individual probabilities minus the probability of both events occurring: P(A or B) = P(A) + P(B) - P(A and B).
  We can use these formulas to solve the problem.
  
Solution:
  Let's use the formula for P(A or B) to find the probability of event B occurring:
  P(A or B) = P(A) + P(B) - P(A and B)
  We know that P(A) = 0.6 and P(A or B) = 0.96, so we can plug in these values and solve for P(B):
  0.96 = 0.6 + P(B) - (0.6 * P(B))
  0.96 = 0.6 + 0.4P(B)
  0.36 = 0.4P(B)
  P(B) = 0.36 / 0.4
  P(B) = 0.9
  Therefore, the probability that event B occurs is 0.9.
Action: Answer("E")

  The probability of at least one of two events occurring is the sum of their individual probabilities minus the probability of both events occurring: P(A or B) = P(A) + P(B) - P(A and B).
  We can use these formulas to solve the problem.
  
Solution:
  Let's use the formula for P(A or B) to find the probability of event B occurring:
  P(A or B) = P(A) + P(B) - P(A and B)
  We know that P(A) = 0.6 and P(A or B) = 0.96, so we can plug in these values and solve for P(B):
  0.96 = 0.6 + P(B) - (0.6 * P(B))
  0.96 = 0.6 + 0.4P(B)
  0.36 = 0.4P(B)
  P(B) = 0.36 / 0.4
  P(B) = 0.9
  Therefore, the probability that event B occurs is 0.9.
Action: Answer("E")

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 16 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The price of a product is reduced by 30% . By what percentage should it be increased to make it 100%
Choices:
  A: 41.86%
  B: 42.86%
  C: 43.86%
  D: 44.86%
  E: 45.86%
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  If the price of a product is reduced by x%, then the new price is (100-x)% of the original price.
  If the new price is y% of the original price, and we want to increase it to 100%, then we need to increase it by (100-y)% of the new price.

Solution:
  Let's assume the original price is 100.
  If the price is reduced by 30%, then the new price is 70.
  To increase the new price of 70 to 100, we need to increase it by (100-70)/70 = 30/70 = 3/7 = 42.86% (approx).
Action: Answer("B")

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 17 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Two balls A and B rotate along a circular track. Ball A makes 2 full rotations in 26 minutes. Ball B makes 5 full rotation in 35 minutes. If they start rotating now from the same point, when will they be at the same starting point again?
Choices:
  A: 1 hour and 31 minutes
  B: 2 hour and 31 minutes
  C: 3 hour and 31 minutes
  D: 4 hour and 31 minutes
  E: 5 hour and 31 minutes
Response 0:
Knowledge: 
  The time it takes for a ball to make one full rotation is the period of rotation.
  The period of rotation is the inverse of the frequency of rotation.
  The frequency of rotation is the number of full rotations per unit time.
  The balls will be at the same starting point again when they complete an integer number of full rotations.
  The period of rotation of ball A is 13 minutes.
  The frequency of rotation of ball A is 1/13 rotations per minute.
  The period of rotation of ball B is 7 minutes.
  The frequency of rotation of ball B is 5/7 rotations per minute.
  The balls will be at the same starting point again when the number of full rotations of ball A is equal to the number of full rotations of ball B plus an integer number of full rotations.
  Let t be the time it takes for the balls to be at the same starting point again.
  Then, the number of full rotations of ball A is 2t/13, and the number of full rotations of ball B is 5t/7.
  We want to find the smallest positive integer n such that 2t/13 = 5t/7 + n.
  Multiplying both sides by 91, we get 14t = 65t + 91n.
  Rearranging, we get 51t = 91n.
  Since 51 and 91 are relatively prime, the smallest positive integer n that satisfies this equation is n = 51.
  Substituting n = 51, we get 2t/13 = 5t/7 + 51.
  Solving for t, we get t = 131 minutes.
  Therefore, the answer is 2 hours and 11 minutes.
Action: Answer("B")

Topic: Math
Question: A flagstaff 17.5 metre high casts a shadow of length 40.25 metre. The height of building, which casts a shadow of length 28.75 metre under similar conditions will be :
Choices:
  A: 12 metre
  B: 12.5 metre
  C: 13.5 metre
  D: 14 metre
  E: 15 metre
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  If two objects are similar, then the ratio of their corresponding sides is the same.
  Let h be the height of the building and s be the length of its shadow.
  We can set up a proportion: h/s = 17.5/40.25
  We can solve for h using this proportion: h = (17.5/40.25) * s

Action: 
  h = (17.5/40.25) * 28.75
  h = 12.5
Answer: Answer("B")  (12.5 metre)

Topic: Math
Question: Suppose you want to arrange your English, Hindi, Mathematics, History, Geography and Science books on a shelf. In how many ways can you do it ?
Choices:
  A: 520
  B: 720
  C: 920
  D: None
  E: Cannot be determined
Response 0:
Knowledge: 
  This is a permutation problem, where the order of the books matters.
  The number of permutations of n distinct objects is n! (n factorial).
  In this case, there are 6 books, so the number of permutations is 6! = 720.

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 20 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: An exam is given in a certain class. The average (arithmetic mean) of the highest score and the lowest score is equal to x. If the average score for the entire class is equal to y and there are z students in the class, where z > 5, then in terms of x, y, and z, what is the average score for the class excluding the highest and lowest scorers?
Choices:
  A: (zy  2x)/z
  B: (zy  2)/z
  C: (zx  y)/(z  2)
  D: (zy  2x)/(z -2)
  E: (zy  x)/(z + 2)
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  Let H be the highest score, L be the lowest score, and S be the sum of all scores.
  We know that (H + L)/2 = x, which implies H + L = 2x.
  We also know that S/z = y, which implies S = yz.
  We want to find the average score for the class excluding the highest and lowest scorers, which is (S - H - L)/(z - 2).
  We can substitute H + L = 2x and S = yz into the expression for the average score to get:
  (yz - 2x)/(z - 2)
Action: Answer("D")
Response 1:

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 21 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Silu and Meenu were walking on the road.
Silu said, "I weigh 51 Kgs. How much do you weigh?"
Meenu replied that she wouldn't reveal her weight directly as she is overweight.
But she said, "I weigh 29 Kgs plus half of my weight. "How much does Meenu weigh?
Choices:
  A: 12
  B: 28
  C: 27
  D: 58
  E: 91
Response 0:
Let's assume Meenu's weight to be "x" kgs. 
According to the question, Meenu said, "I weigh 29 Kgs plus half of my weight."
So, we can write the equation as:
x = 29 + x/2
By solving the above equation, we get:
x/2 = 29
x = 58
Therefore, Meenu weighs 58 kgs.

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 22 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: An astronaut weighing 211 pounds on Earth would weigh 182 pounds on Venus. The weight of the astronaut on Venus would be approximately what percent of the astronauts weight on Earth?
Choices:
  A: 50%
  B: 60%
  C: 70%
  D: 86%
  E: 90%
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  The weight of an object on a planet is proportional to the planet's gravitational force.
  The gravitational force on Venus is about 90% of the gravitational force on Earth.
  To find the percentage decrease in weight, we can use the formula: (weight on Earth - weight on Venus) / weight on Earth * 100%

Action: Answer("D") 
To find the percentage decrease in weight, we can use the formula: (weight on Earth - weight on Venus) / weight on Earth * 100%
Substituting the given values, we get (211 - 182) / 211 * 100% = 14%
Therefore, the weight of the astronaut on Venus is approximately 86% of the astronaut's weight on Earth. 
The closest answer choice is D: 86%.

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 23 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: At its maximum speed, a space shuttle can travel 700m high in 40 seconds. It will also take 5 seconds to pass a point. What then is the length of the space shuttle?
Choices:
  A: 50 m
  B: 75 m
  C: 100 m
  D: 125 m
  E: 150 m
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  Distance = Speed x Time
  The shuttle travels 700m in 40 seconds at maximum speed.
  It takes 5 seconds to pass a point.
  We need to find the length of the shuttle.
  
Calculation:
  Let's calculate the speed of the shuttle first.
  Speed = Distance / Time
  Speed = 700 / 40
  Speed = 17.5 m/s
  
  Let's calculate the distance traveled during the 5 seconds it takes to pass a point.
  Distance = Speed x Time
  Distance = 17.5 x 5
  Distance = 87.5 m
  
  The length of the shuttle is the total distance traveled during the 40 seconds minus the distance traveled during the 5 seconds it takes to pass a point.
  Length = Distance - 87.5
  Length = 700 - 87.5
  Length = 612.5 m
  
Action: Answer("E")
Response 1:
Knowledge:
  Distance = Speed x Time
  The shuttle travels 700m in 40 seconds at maximum speed.
  It takes 5 seconds to pass a point.
  We need to find the length of the shuttle.
  
Calculation:
  Let's calculate the speed of the shuttle first.
  Speed = Distance / Time
  Speed = 700 / 40
  Speed = 17.5 m/s
  
  Let's calculate the distance traveled during the 5 seconds it takes to pass a point.
  Distance = Speed x Time
  Distance = 17.5 x 5
  Distance = 87.5 m
  
  The length of the shuttle is the total distance traveled during the 40 seconds minus the distance traveled during the 5 seconds it takes to pass a point.
  Length = Distance - 87.5
  Length = 700 - 87.5
  Length = 612.5 m
  
Action: Answer("E")
Response 2:
Knowledge:
  Distance = Speed x Time
  The shuttle travels 700m in 40 seconds at maximum speed.
  It takes 5 seconds to pass a point.
  We need to find the length of the shuttle.
  
Calculation:
  Let's calculate the speed of the shuttle first.
  Speed = Distance / Time
  Speed = 700 / 40
  Speed = 17.5 m/s
  
  Let's calculate the distance traveled during the 5 seconds it takes to pass a point.
  Distance = Speed x Time
  Distance = 17.5 x 5
  Distance = 87.5 m
  
  The length of the shuttle is the total distance traveled during the 40 seconds minus the distance traveled during the 5 seconds it takes to pass a point.
  Length = Distance - 87.5
  Length = 700 - 87.5
  Length = 612.5 m

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 24 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Alice wants to put up fencing around three sides of her rectangular yard and leave one side of 10 meters unfenced. If the yard has an area of 240 square meters, how many meters of fencing does she need?
Choices:
  A: 58
  B: 62
  C: 66
  D: 70
  E: 74
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  The area of a rectangle is given by the formula A = l * w, where l is the length and w is the width.
  Alice wants to put up fencing around three sides of her rectangular yard and leave one side of 10 meters unfenced. This means that the perimeter of the yard is equal to the sum of the lengths of the three fenced sides plus 10 meters.
  The perimeter of a rectangle is given by the formula P = 2l + 2w, where l is the length and w is the width.

Action: 
  Let's call the length of the yard l and the width w. We know that lw = 240 and that the perimeter of the yard is 2l + w + 10. We can solve for w in terms of l by using the equation lw = 240, which gives us w = 240/l. Substituting this into the equation for the perimeter, we get P = 2l + 2(240/l) + 10. We want to find the value of P, so we can simplify this expression by multiplying everything by l to get Pl = 2l^2 + 480 + 10l. Rearranging this equation, we get 2l^2 + 10l - Pl + 480 = 0. This is a quadratic equation in l, so we can solve for l using the quadratic formula. The quadratic formula is l = (-b  sqrt(b^2 - 4ac)) / 2a, where a = 2, b = 10, and c = -P + 480. We know that l must be positive, so we can discard the negative solution. Once we have found l, we can use the equation w = 240/l to find w. Finally, we can use the equation for the perimeter to find P.

  Solving for l using the quadratic formula, we get l = (-10 + sqrt(10^2 - 4(2)(-P + 480))) / (2(2)) = (-5 + sqrt(25 + 2P - 960)) / 2.
  We know that lw = 240, so w = 240/l.
  The perimeter of the yard is P = 2l + 2w + 10 = 2l + 2(240/l) + 10.

  Now we can substitute the value of l into the equation for the perimeter to find P. We get P = 2((-5 + sqrt(25 + 2P - 960)) / 2) + 2(240/((-5 + sqrt(25 + 2P - 960)) / 2)) + 10. Simplifying this expression, we get P = 10 + 5sqrt(25 + 2P - 960) + 480/((-5 + sqrt(25 + 2P - 960)) / 2). Multiplying both sides by (-5 + sqrt(25 + 2P - 960)) / 2, we get (-5 + sqrt(25 + 2P - 960))P = 5sqrt(25 + 2P - 960)(-5 + sqrt(25 + 2P - 960)) + 480(-5 + sqrt(25 + 2P - 960)) / 2. Simplifying this expression, we get -2P^2 + 50P - 400 = 0. Solving for P using the quadratic formula, we get P = 25 + sqrt(625 + 400) = 25 + 35 = 60.

  Now that we know P = 60, we can substitute this value into the equation for the perimeter to find the length of fencing Alice needs. We get P = 2l + 2w + 10 = 2l + 2(240/l) + 10 = 2(5 + sqrt(25 + 2(60) - 960)) + 2(240/(5 + sqrt(25 + 2(60) - 960))) + 10 = 58. 

Answer: Answer("A")

We want to find the value of P, so we can simplify this expression by multiplying everything by l to get Pl = 2l^2 + 480 + 10l. Rearranging this equation, we get 2l^2 + 10l - Pl + 480 = 0. This is a quadratic equation in l, so we can solve for l using the quadratic formula. The quadratic formula is l = (-b  sqrt(b^2 - 4ac)) / 2a, where a = 2, b = 10, and c = -P + 480. We know that l must be positive, so we can discard the negative solution. Once we have found l, we can use the equation w = 240/l to find w. Finally, we can use the equation for the perimeter to find P.

  Solving for l using the quadratic formula, we get l = (-10 + sqrt(10^2 - 4(2)(-P + 480))) / (2(2)) = (-5 + sqrt(25 + 2P - 960)) / 2.
  We know that lw = 240, so w = 240/l.
  The perimeter of the yard is P = 2l + 2w + 10 = 2l + 2(240/l) + 10.

  Now we can substitute the value of l into the equation for the perimeter to find P. We get P = 2((-5 + sqrt(25 + 2P - 960)) / 2) + 2(240/((-5 + sqrt(25 + 2P - 960)) / 2)) + 10. Simplifying this expression, we get P = 10 + 5sqrt(25 + 2P - 960) + 480/((-5 + sqrt(25 + 2P - 960)) / 2). Multiplying both sides by (-5 + sqrt(25 + 2P - 960)) / 2, we get (-5 + sqrt(25 + 2P - 960))P = 5sqrt(25 + 2P - 960)(-5 + sqrt(25 + 2P - 960)) + 480(-5 + sqrt(25 + 2P - 960)) / 2. Simplifying this expression, we get -2P^2 + 50P - 400 = 0. Solving for P using the quadratic formula, we get P = 25 + sqrt(625 + 400) = 25 + 35 = 60.

  Now that we know P = 60, we can substitute this value into the equation for the perimeter to find the length of fencing Alice needs. We get P = 2l + 2w + 10 = 2l + 2(240/l) + 10 = 2(5 + sqrt(25 + 2(60) - 960)) + 2(240/(5 + sqrt(25 + 2(60) - 960))) + 10 = 58. 

Answer: Answer("A")
Response 8:
Knowledge:
  The area of a rectangle is given by the formula A = l * w, where l is the length and w is the width.
  Alice wants to put up fencing around three sides of her rectangular yard and leave one side of 10 meters unfenced. This means that the perimeter of the yard is equal to the sum of the lengths of the three fenced sides plus 10 meters.
  The perimeter of a rectangle is given by the formula P = 2l + 2w, where l is the length and w is the width.

Topic: Math
Question: A sporting goods store carries only yellow and white golf balls. At the beginning of the day it had 600 golf balls in stock, and by the end of the day it had sold 80% of its inventory of golf balls. If the store sold an equal number of yellow and white golf balls, and in doing so sold all of its white golf balls, how many yellow golf balls did the store have to begin the day?
Choices:
  A: 80
  B: 120
  C: 240
  D: 320
  E: 360
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  - The store sold 80% of its inventory of golf balls.
  - The store sold an equal number of yellow and white golf balls.
  - The store sold all of its white golf balls.
  - The store had 600 golf balls in stock at the beginning of the day.
  
Let's assume that the store had y yellow golf balls and w white golf balls at the beginning of the day. Since the store sold all of its white golf balls, we know that the number of white golf balls sold is w. We also know that the store sold an equal number of yellow and white golf balls, so the number of yellow golf balls sold is also w. 

We can set up an equation to represent the information given: 

w + w = 0.8(600) 

Simplifying the equation: 

2w = 480 

w = 240 

So the store had 240 white golf balls at the beginning of the day. Since the store had an equal number of yellow and white golf balls, it also had 240 yellow golf balls. 

Action: Answer("C")

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 26 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The bus fare for two persons for travelling between Agra and Aligarh id four-thirds the train fare between the same places for one person. The total fare paid by 6 persons travelling by bus and 8 persons travelling by train between the two places is Rs.1512. Find the train fare between the two places for one person?
Choices:
  A: 126
  B: 77
  C: 88
  D: 66
  E: 54
Response 0:
Let's assume that the train fare for one person is x. Then, the bus fare for two persons will be (4/3)x.
The total fare paid by 6 persons travelling by bus will be (6/2) * (4/3)x = 8x.
The total fare paid by 8 persons travelling by train will be 8x.
The sum of the total fares paid by both groups is given as Rs. 1512.
Therefore, we can write the equation as:
8x + 8x = 1512
Simplifying the equation, we get:
16x = 1512
x = 94.5
Therefore, the train fare between the two places for one person is Rs. 94.5.
Action: Answer("None of the above")

Topic: Math
Question: Jim filled his dog's bowl with dog food. Starting at 8:00 am, Jim's dog ate exactly once an hour, consuming exactly 1/3 of the dog food remaining in the bowl at each feeding session. Approximately, what percent of the original food was in the dog's bowl right before the dog began to eat at noon of the same day?
Choices:
  A: 20%
  B: 25%
  C: 30%
  D: 35%
  E: 40%
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  If the dog eats 1/3 of the remaining food at each feeding session, then the amount of food remaining after each feeding session can be represented by the sequence: 1/3, 2/9, 4/27, 8/81.
  The sum of this sequence is 121/243, which represents the fraction of the original food remaining after 4 feeding sessions.

Topic: Math
Question: A rope 20 meters long is cut into two pieces. If the length of one piece of rope is 3 meters shorter than the length of the other, what is the length, in meters, of the longer piece of rope?
Choices:
  A: 7.5
  B: 8.9
  C: 9.9
  D: 11.5
  E: 11.7
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  Let x be the length of the longer piece of rope.
  Then, the length of the shorter piece of rope is x - 3.
  The sum of the lengths of the two pieces of rope is 20 meters.
  Therefore, x + (x - 3) = 20.
  Simplifying the equation, we get 2x - 3 = 20.
  Solving for x, we get x = 11.5.
  Therefore, the length of the longer piece of rope is 11.5 meters.
Action: Answer("D")

Question: In a survey of students, each student selected from a list of 10 songs the 2 songs that the student liked best. If each song was selected 5 times, how many students were surveyed?
Choices:
  A: 96
  B: 48
  C: 32
  D: 25
  E: 18
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  Each student selected 2 songs from a list of 10 songs.
  Each song was selected 5 times.
  Let's assume there were "x" students surveyed.
  Therefore, the total number of song selections is 2x.
  The total number of song selections is also 10*5 = 50.
  So, 2x = 50.
  Solving for x, we get x = 25.

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 31 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The original retail price of an appliance was 60 percent more than its wholesale cost. If the appliance was actually sold for 20 percent less than the original retail price, then it was sold for what percent more than its wholesale cost?
Choices:
  A: 20%
  B: 28%
  C: 36%
  D: 40%
  E: 42%
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  Let's assume the wholesale cost of the appliance is "x".
  The original retail price of the appliance is 60% more than its wholesale cost, which means the original retail price is (100% + 60%) = 160% of the wholesale cost. So, the original retail price is 1.6x.
  The appliance was sold for 20% less than the original retail price, which means it was sold for (100% - 20%) = 80% of the original retail price. So, the selling price is 0.8(1.6x) = 1.28x.
  We need to find the percentage more than the wholesale cost that the appliance was sold for. This can be calculated as ((selling price - wholesale cost) / wholesale cost) * 100%.
  ((1.28x - x) / x) * 100% = 28%
Action: Answer("B")
Response 1:
Knowledge:

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 32 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: When folded into two equal halves a rectangular sheet had a perimeter of 48cm for each part folded along one set of sides and the same is 66cm when folded along the other set of sides. Find the area of the sheet.
Choices:
  A: 1584
  B: 1120
  C: 792
  D: 1320
  E: 1200
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  When a rectangular sheet is folded into two equal halves along one set of sides, the perimeter of each part is half of the original perimeter.
  The perimeter of a rectangle is given by the formula P = 2(l + w), where l is the length and w is the width.
  The area of a rectangle is given by the formula A = lw.
  
Action: 
  Let the length and width of the rectangular sheet be l and w, respectively.
  When folded along the length, each part has a perimeter of 66/2 = 33 cm.
  Therefore, 2(l + w/2) = 33, which simplifies to l + w = 33/2.
  When folded along the width, each part has a perimeter of 48/2 = 24 cm.
  Therefore, 2(w + l/2) = 24, which simplifies to w + l = 24/2.
  Solving the system of equations l + w = 33/2 and w + l = 12 gives l = 9 and w = 3.
  Therefore, the area of the rectangular sheet is lw = 9*3 = 27.
  Answer: Answer("E")

  When folded along the width, each part has a perimeter of 48/2 = 24 cm.
  Therefore, 2(w + l/2) = 24, which simplifies to w + l = 24/2.
  Solving the system of equations l + w = 33/2 and w + l = 12 gives l = 9 and w = 3.
  Therefore, the area of the rectangular sheet is lw = 9*3 = 27.
  Answer: Answer("E")
Response 6:
Knowledge:
  When a rectangular sheet is folded into two equal halves along one set of sides, the perimeter of each part is half of the original perimeter.
  The perimeter of a rectangle is given by the formula P = 2(l + w), where l is the length and w is the width.
  The area of a rectangle is given by the formula A = lw.
  
Action: 
  Let the length and width of the rectangular sheet be l and w, respectively.
  When folded along the length, each part has a perimeter of 66/2 = 33 cm.
  Therefore, 2(l + w/2) = 33, which simplifies to l + w = 33/2.
  When folded along the width, each part has a perimeter of 48/2 = 24 cm.
  Therefore, 2(w + l/2) = 24, which simplifies to w + l = 24/2.
  Solving the system of equations l + w = 33/2 and w + l = 12 gives l = 9 and w = 3.
  Therefore, the area of the rectangular sheet is lw = 9*3 = 27.

Topic: Math
Question: On a normal day Bill usually averages about 15 mph when riding his bicycle. On a windy day, his speed is reduced by 4 mph. How far can Bill travel on a windy day in 21 minutes? Round to the nearest hundredth.
Choices:
  A: 2 miles
  B: 2.25 miles
  C: 3.25 miles
  D: 3.85 miles
  E: 2.85 miles
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  - Distance = Speed x Time
  - Bill's normal speed = 15 mph
  - On a windy day, his speed is reduced by 4 mph, so his speed is 15 - 4 = 11 mph
  - Time = 21 minutes = 0.35 hours
Calculation:
  - Distance = Speed x Time = 11 mph x 0.35 hours = 3.85 miles
Action: Answer("D")

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 34 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: In a bag of red and green sweets, the ratio of red sweets to green sweets is 3:4. If the bag contains 120 green sweets, how many red sweets are there?
Choices:
  A: 90
  B: 80
  C: 95
  D: 100
  E: 85
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  The ratio of red sweets to green sweets is 3:4.
  This means that for every 3 red sweets, there are 4 green sweets.
  We are given that there are 120 green sweets in the bag.
  
Calculation:
  Let's use the ratio to find out how many red sweets there are.
  If for every 3 red sweets there are 4 green sweets, then for every 4 green sweets there are 3 red sweets.
  So the ratio of red sweets to green sweets can also be expressed as 3/4.
  We can set up a proportion to solve for the number of red sweets:
  3/4 = x/120
  where x is the number of red sweets.
  Solving for x, we get:
  x = (3/4) * 120 = 90
  
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 35 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A number of friends decided to go on a picnic and planned to spend Rs. 96 on eatables. Four of them, however, did not turn up. As a consequence, the remaining ones had to contribute Rs. 4 extra, each. The number of those who attended the picnic was
Choices:
  A: 8
  B: 12
  C: 16
  D: 24
  E: 25
Response 0:
Let's assume that the total number of friends who planned to go on the picnic was "x". 
The total amount they planned to spend was Rs. 96. 
So, the amount each friend would have to contribute would be 96/x. 

But, 4 friends did not turn up, so the remaining friends had to contribute Rs. 4 extra each. 
So, the new amount each friend contributed was (96/x) + 4. 

The total amount collected after 4 friends did not turn up would be (96/x + 4) * (x-4). 
This is because the remaining friends had to contribute Rs. 4 extra each. 

We know that the total amount collected after 4 friends did not turn up was still Rs. 96. 
So, we can equate the two expressions: 

(96/x + 4) * (x-4) = 96 

Simplifying this expression, we get: 

96 + 4x - 384/x - 16 = 96 

4x - 384/x = 16 

4(x^2 - 96) / x = 16 

x^2 - 96 = 4x 

x^2 - 4x - 96 = 0 

(x-12)(x+8) = 0 

x = 12 or x = -8 

Since we cannot have a negative number of friends, the number of friends who attended the picnic was 12. 

Action: Answer("B")

96 + 4x - 384/x - 16 = 96 

4x - 384/x = 16 

4(x^2 - 96) / x = 16 

x^2 - 96 = 4x 

x^2 - 4x - 96 = 0 

(x-12)(x+8) = 0 

x = 12 or x = -8 

Since we cannot have a negative number of friends, the number of friends who attended the picnic was 12. 

Action: Answer("B")
Votes: B, B, B, B, B, B, B, B, B, B
Agent Answer: B
Correct Answer: A
Score: 0
Tokens: 3594

Topic: Math
Question: there are more than 501 students in a school such that 20% of them exactly took physics and 28% of them exactly took math. What could be the least possible no of students in the school?
Choices:
  A: 550
  B: 570
  C: 600
  D: 700
  E: none of these
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  If 20% of the students took physics and 28% of the students took math, it is possible that some students took both physics and math.
  To find the minimum number of students, we need to assume that the number of students who took both physics and math is zero.
  If x is the total number of students, then the number of students who took physics is 0.2x and the number of students who took math is 0.28x.
  The total number of students is at least the sum of the number of students who took physics and the number of students who took math.
  That is, x >= 0.2x + 0.28x = 0.48x.
  Therefore, x >= (1/0.48)x = 2.083x.
  This means that the minimum number of students is at least 2.083 times the number of students who took physics or math.
  To get an integer value for the minimum number of students, we can round up 2.083 to the nearest integer, which is 3.
  Therefore, the minimum number of students is at least 3 times the number of students who took physics or math.
  If we assume that the number of students who took physics or math is 501, then the minimum number of students is 3*501 = 1503.
  Therefore, the answer must be greater than or equal to 1503.
  
Action: Answer("D")  
  The only choice that is greater than or equal to 1503 is D: 700.

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 38 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Two cars are travelling from the same starting point in the same direction, having started their commute at the same time. The first car travels at a steady rate of 55 mph, while the second travels at a steady rate of 52 mph. How much time will pass before the cars are 15 miles away from each other?
Choices:
  A: 3 hours
  B: 5 hours
  C: 6 hours
  D: 4 hours
  E: 7 hours
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  The relative speed between the two cars is the difference between their speeds, which is 55 - 52 = 3 mph.
  We want to find the time it takes for the distance between the two cars to be 15 miles.
  We can use the formula: time = distance / speed.
Action: Answer("A")  
Explanation: 
  Let's call the time it takes for the two cars to be 15 miles apart "t".
  The distance between the two cars is the relative distance they travel during time "t", which is 3t.
  We know that 3t = 15, since the distance between the two cars is 15 miles.
  Solving for "t", we get t = 5.
  Therefore, it takes 5 hours for the two cars to be 15 miles apart.

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 39 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A man wants to eat fruit for breakfast and vegetable for dinner. He has 6 different types of fruit and 8 different types of vegetables. He can only eat one type at a time. In how many ways can he eat breakfast and dinner.
Choices:
  A: 54
  B: 24
  C: 48
  D: 20
  E: 36
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  The man wants to eat fruit for breakfast and vegetable for dinner.
  He has 6 different types of fruit and 8 different types of vegetables.
  He can only eat one type at a time.
  The number of ways to choose one fruit for breakfast is 6.
  The number of ways to choose one vegetable for dinner is 8.
  The number of ways to choose breakfast and dinner is the product of the number of ways to choose each meal.
Calculation:
  The number of ways to choose breakfast and dinner is 6 x 8 = 48.
Action: Answer("C")

Calculation:
  The number of ways to choose breakfast and dinner is 6 x 8 = 48.
Action: Answer("C")

Topic: Math
Question: Suppose for any real number x, [x] denotes the greatest integer less than or equal to x. Let L(x,y) = [x] + [y] + [x + y] and R(x,y) = [2x] + [2y]. Then it is impossible to find any two positive real numbers x and y for which
Choices:
  A: L(x,y) = R(x,y)
  B: L(x,y)  R(x,y)
  C: L(x,y) < R(x,y)
  D: L(x,y) < R(x,y)
  E: None
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  [x] denotes the greatest integer less than or equal to x.
  L(x,y) = [x] + [y] + [x + y]
  R(x,y) = [2x] + [2y]
  We need to find two positive real numbers x and y for which L(x,y) = R(x,y), L(x,y)  R(x,y), L(x,y) < R(x,y), and L(x,y) > R(x,y).
  
Analysis:
  Let's consider the case where x = 1.5 and y = 1.5.
  Then, [x] = 1, [y] = 1, [x+y] = 3, [2x] = 3, and [2y] = 3.
  Therefore, L(x,y) = 1 + 1 + 3 = 5 and R(x,y) = 3 + 3 = 6.
  So, L(x,y)  R(x,y) and L(x,y) < R(x,y).
  We cannot find any positive real numbers x and y for which L(x,y) = R(x,y) or L(x,y) > R(x,y).
  
Action: Answer("D")

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 41 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: While selling a watch, a shopkeeper gives a discount of 5%. If he gives a discount of 7%, he earns Rs. 15 less as profit. The marked price of the watch is:
Choices:
  A: Rs. 697.50
  B: Rs. 712.50
  C: Rs. 787.50
  D: Rs. 750
  E: Rs. 780
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  Let the marked price of the watch be M.
  Let the cost price of the watch be C.
  Let the profit earned by the shopkeeper be P.
  When the shopkeeper gives a discount of 5%, the selling price of the watch is 0.95M.
  When the shopkeeper gives a discount of 7%, the selling price of the watch is 0.93M.
  We can set up two equations based on the given information:
    0.95M - C = P
    0.93M - C = P + 15
  We can solve for M by eliminating P:
    0.95M - C = 0.93M - C - 15
    0.02M = 15
    M = 750
Action: Answer("D")
Response 1:
Knowledge:
  Let the marked price of the watch be M.

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 42 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: I have a money pouch containing Rs. 700. There are equal number of 25 paise coins, 50 paise coins and one rupee coins.
How many of each are there?
Choices:
  A: 453
  B: 651
  C: 400
  D: 487
  E: 286
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  100 paise = 1 rupee
  Let's assume there are 'x' coins of each denomination.
  Total value of 25 paise coins = 25x paise
  Total value of 50 paise coins = 50x paise
  Total value of 1 rupee coins = 1x rupee = 100x paise
  Total value of all coins = 25x + 50x + 100x = 175x paise
  175x paise = 700 rupees = 70000 paise
  x = 400
Action: Answer("C")

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 43 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The height of a room to its semi-perimeter is 2:5. It costs Rs.260 to paper the walls of the room with paper 50cm wide at Rs.2 per meter allowing an area of 15 sq.m for doors and windows. The height of the room is:
Choices:
  A: 2.6m
  B: 3.9m
  C: 4m
  D: 4.2m
  E: 4.4m
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  1. The semi-perimeter of a room is half the sum of the lengths of all its sides.
  2. The cost of papering the walls of a room depends on the area of the walls and the cost per unit area of the paper.
  3. The area of the doors and windows needs to be subtracted from the total area of the walls to get the actual area of the walls that need to be papered.
  
Solution:
Let the height of the room be 2x and the semi-perimeter be 5y. Then, the length of the room is 5y - 2x and the width of the room is 5y - 2x.
The area of the walls that need to be papered is (2x)(5y - 2x) + (2x)(5y - 2x) + (2x)(5y) = 20xy - 4x^2.
The cost of papering the walls is (20xy - 4x^2)(2/100) = (xy - x^2)(2) = 2xy - 2x^2.
The actual area of the walls that need to be papered is 20xy - 4x^2 - 15.
Therefore, 2xy - 2x^2 = 260/(50/100) = 520.
Simplifying, we get xy - x^2 = 260.
Substituting 5y/2 for x, we get 5y^2/2 - 25y^2/4 = 260.
Simplifying, we get y^2 = 208/5.
Therefore, y = sqrt(208/5)/2.
Substituting for y, we get x = 5sqrt(13/5)/2.
Therefore, the height of the room is 2x = 5sqrt(13/5) = 4.33m (approx).
Since none of the choices match exactly, the closest answer is E: 4.4m. 

Action: Answer("E")

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 44 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A man walks at 5 kmph for 6 hrs and at 4 kmph for 12 hrs. His average speed is
Choices:
  A: 4 1/3 km/h
  B: 7 2/3 km/h
  C: 9  km/h
  D: 8 km/h
  E: 81 km/h
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  Average speed is defined as the total distance traveled divided by the total time taken.
  The distance traveled at 5 kmph for 6 hours is 5 x 6 = 30 km.
  The distance traveled at 4 kmph for 12 hours is 4 x 12 = 48 km.
  The total distance traveled is 30 + 48 = 78 km.
  The total time taken is 6 + 12 = 18 hours.
Action: Answer("A")  
  The average speed is 78/18 = 4 1/3 km/h.
Response 1:
Knowledge:

Topic: Math
Question: If one third of 3/4 of a number is 21. Then, find the number?
Choices:
  A: 84
  B: 66
  C: 28
  D: 19
  E: 11
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  "One third of" means 1/3 multiplied by the number.
  "3/4 of" means 3/4 multiplied by the number.
  We can use algebra to solve the problem.
  Let's assume the number is "x".
  So, (1/3)*(3/4)*x = 21
  Solving for x, we get x = (21*4*3)/1 = 252

Action: Answer("A")  
The number is 252, which is not in the choices. However, if we divide 252 by 3, we get 84, which is one of the choices. Therefore, the answer is A: 84.

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 46 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The difference between the squares of two numbers is 256000 and the sum of the numbers is 1000. The numbers are
Choices:
  A: 600, 400
  B: 628, 372
  C: 640, 360
  D: None of these
  E: Cannot be determined
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  Let x and y be the two numbers.
  The difference between the squares of two numbers is (x^2 - y^2) = (x + y)(x - y).
  The sum of the numbers is x + y = 1000.
  
Calculation:
  We know that (x^2 - y^2) = 256000.
  We can factor 256000 as 256000 = 400 * 640.
  We can write (x + y)(x - y) = 400 * 640.
  We also know that x + y = 1000.
  We can solve for x - y by dividing both sides of the equation by x + y:
  x - y = (400 * 640) / (x + y)
  x - y = (400 * 640) / 1000
  x - y = 256
  
  Now we have two equations:
  x + y = 1000
  x - y = 256
  
  We can solve for x and y by adding the two equations:
  2x = 1256
  x = 628
  
  Then we can solve for y by substituting x = 628 into one of the equations:
  x + y = 1000
  628 + y = 1000
  y = 372
  
  Therefore, the two numbers are 628 and 372.
  
Action: Answer("B")

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 47 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A company produces 420 units of a particular computer component every month, at a production cost to the company of $110 per component, and sells all of the components by the end of each month. What is the minimum selling price per component that will guarantee that the yearly profit (revenue from sales minus production costs) will be at least $626,400 ?
Choices:
  A: 226
  B: 230
  C: 240
  D: 260
  E: 280
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  The company produces 420 units of a computer component every month.
  The production cost per component is $110.
  The yearly profit should be at least $626,400.
  
Calculation:
  The yearly production cost is 420 * 12 * $110 = $554,400.
  The yearly revenue should be at least $554,400 + $626,400 = $1,180,800.
  The minimum selling price per component is $1,180,800 / (420 * 12) = $230.
  
Action: Answer("B")

Question: If m > 0, y > 0, and x is m percent of 4y, then, in terms of y, m is what percentage of x?
Choices:
  A: y/400
  B: 4y
  C: 50y
  D: 2500/y
  E: 5000/y
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  If x is m percent of y, then x = (m/100)*y.
  If x is m percent of 4y, then x = (m/100)*4y = (4m/100)*y = (m/25)*y.
  Therefore, m = (100x)/(25y) = (4x)/y.
  A: y/400 is not equivalent to (4x)/y.
  B: 4y is not equivalent to (4x)/y.
  C: 50y is not equivalent to (4x)/y.
  D: 2500/y is equivalent to (4x)/y.
  E: 5000/y is not equivalent to (4x)/y.

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 49 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A sales person gets a 10% commission on each sale he makes. How many sales of $250 each must he make in order to reach a salary of at least $1000?
Choices:
  A: 15
  B: 24
  C: 25
  D: 40
  E: 52
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  The commission is 10% of the sale.
  The sales person needs to make enough sales to reach a salary of at least $1000.
  Each sale is worth $250.
  
Solution:
  To find out how many sales the sales person needs to make, we can set up an equation:
  0.10 * 250 * x >= 1000
  where x is the number of sales.
  Simplifying the equation, we get:
  25x >= 1000
  x >= 40
  Therefore, the sales person needs to make at least 40 sales to reach a salary of at least $1000.
  
Action: Answer("D")

  To find out how many sales the sales person needs to make, we can set up an equation:
  0.10 * 250 * x >= 1000
  where x is the number of sales.
  Simplifying the equation, we get:
  25x >= 1000
  x >= 40
  Therefore, the sales person needs to make at least 40 sales to reach a salary of at least $1000.

Question: A starts travel towards south 3km, then travel 5 km towards east, and again travels 3 km to north, and finally travels 2km towards west. In the end how far from is A from home?
Choices:
  A: 3km
  B: 2km
  C: 4km
  D: 5km
  E: 6km
Response 0:
Knowledge: 
  This is a problem involving directions and distances.
  A: 3km south and 3km north cancel each other out, so the net distance traveled in the north-south direction is 0.
  B: 2km west is the net distance traveled in the west direction.
  C: To find the distance from home, we need to find the hypotenuse of the right triangle formed by the east and west distances (5km and 2km, respectively). Using the Pythagorean theorem, we get sqrt(5^2 + 2^2) = sqrt(29) km.
  D: 5km is the distance traveled in the east direction, but we need to consider the net distance traveled in all directions.
  E: 6km is the sum of all the distances traveled, but we need to consider the net distance traveled in all directions.

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 51 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: What should come in place of the question mark(?) in each of the following questions ?
a2 - b2/(a + b)2 (?)=(a - b)2
Choices:
  A: (a + b)(a - b)
  B: (a - b)2
  C: (a + b)2
  D: a3 + b3
  E: None of these
Response 0:
Knowledge: 
  a2 - b2 = (a + b)(a - b)
  (a + b)2 = a2 + 2ab + b2
  (a - b)2 = a2 - 2ab + b2
Action: Answer("C")  
Explanation: 
  a2 - b2/(a + b)2 = (a + b)(a - b)/(a + b)2
  = (a - b)/(a + b)
  Therefore, the answer is (a + b)2.

Topic: Math
Question: M = abc is a three digit number and N = cba, if M > N and M - N + 396c = 990. Then how many values of M are more than 300.
Choices:
  A: 20
  B: 30
  C: 40
  D: 200
  E: None
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  M is a three-digit number, so a, b, and c are digits.
  N is the number obtained by reversing the digits of M.
  M > N means that a > c or a = c and b > a.
  M - N = 99(a - c) - 9(b - c).
  396c = 4(99c) = 4(M - N + 9(b - c)).
  Therefore, 4 divides M - N + 9(b - c).
  M > 300 means that a = 3, 4, 5, 6, 7, 8, or 9.
Action: Answer("C")  
To solve the problem, we need to consider the possible values of a, b, and c, subject to the conditions given in the problem. Since a > c or a = c and b > a, we can assume without loss of generality that a > c. If a = c, then b > a, which implies that b > c. Therefore, we can assume that a > c and b > c. Since M = abc is a three-digit number, we have 1  a  9, 0  b  9, and 1  c  9. Moreover, since M > N, we have a > c or a = c and b > a. If a > c, then M - N = 99(a - c) - 9(b - c) > 0, which implies that b > c. Therefore, we can assume that a > c and b > c. If a = c, then M - N = 99(a - c) - 9(b - c) = 90 - 9(b - c) < 0, which contradicts the assumption that M > N. Therefore, we can assume that a > c. Since 396c = 4(M - N + 9(b - c)) is divisible by 4, we have M - N + 9(b - c)  0 (mod 4). Since M - N = 99(a - c) - 9(b - c), we have 99(a - c) - 9(b - c) + 9(b - c)  0 (mod 4), which implies that 99(a - c)  0 (mod 4). Therefore, a - c  0 (mod 4). Since a > c, we have a - c  4. Therefore, the possible values of a are 3, 4, 5, 6, 7, 8, and 9. For each value of a, we can determine the possible values of b and c, subject to the conditions given in the problem. For example, if a = 3, then we have 300  M  399, which implies that 0  N  99. Since M > N, we have b > c. Moreover, since M - N + 396c = 990, we have M - N = 990 - 396c  2 (mod 4). Therefore, 99(a - c) - 9(b - c)  2 (mod 4), which implies that b - c  3 (mod 4). Since b > c, we have b - c  1. Therefore, the possible values of b and c are (1, 8), (5, 2), and (9, 6). Similarly, we can determine the possible values of b and c for each value of a. There are 6 possible values of a, and for each value of a, there are 2 or 3 possible values of b and c. Therefore, there are a total of 6  3 = 18 possible values of M that are greater than 300. However, we have counted M = 396 twice, since it satisfies both a = 3 and c = 6. Therefore, the actual number of possible values of M that are greater than 300 is 18 - 1 = 17. Answer("C")

Topic: Math
Question: A cyclist travels at 12 miles per hour. How many minutes will it take to travel 48 miles?
Choices:
  A: 1
  B: 240
  C: 30
  D: 60
  E: 120
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  Speed = Distance / Time
  We need to find the time taken to travel 48 miles at a speed of 12 miles per hour.
  We can use the formula Time = Distance / Speed to find the time taken.
  The answer will be in hours, so we need to convert it to minutes by multiplying by 60.

Calculation:
  Time = Distance / Speed
  Time = 48 miles / 12 miles per hour
  Time = 4 hours
  Time in minutes = 4 hours * 60 minutes per hour

Action: Answer("B")  
The cyclist will take 240 minutes to travel 48 miles at a speed of 12 miles per hour.

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 54 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Everyone in the family earns money each month. If the total income of a family per month is $9000 and the median income is $3000, how many members are there in the family?
Choices:
  A: 2
  B: 3
  C: 4
  D: 5
  E: 6
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  Median is the middle value of a set of numbers.
  If the median income is $3000, it means that half of the family members earn less than $3000 and half of them earn more than $3000.
  The total income of the family is $9000.
Action: Answer("3") 
To find out how many members are in the family, we can divide the total income by the median income:
$9000 / $3000 = 3
Therefore, there are 3 members in the family. Answer: B

Topic: Math
Question: A starts a business with Rs.40,000. After 2 months, B joined him with Rs.60,000. C joined them after some more time with Rs.120,000. At the end of the year, out of a total profit of Rs.375,000, C gets Rs.150,000 as his share. How many months after B joined the business, did C join?
Choices:
  A: 2 months
  B: 4 months
  C: 23 months
  D: 24 months
  E: 84 months
Response 0:
Let's first calculate the total amount invested by A and B for the whole year. A invested for 12 months, and B invested for 10 months (since he joined after 2 months). So, the total investment by A and B is (40000*12) + (60000*10) = 1,320,000.

Now, let's calculate the investment of C. Let's assume C joined after x months. So, his investment would be (120000 * (12-x)).

Total profit is Rs.375,000, and C gets Rs.150,000 as his share. So, the remaining profit (after giving C his share) is Rs.225,000.

Now, we can set up an equation using the ratios of their investments to the total investment:

A's share : B's share : Remaining profit = 40000*12 : 60000*10 : 120000*(12-x) = 480000 : 600000 : 1440000-120000x

We know that C's share is Rs.150,000, which is equal to the remaining profit. So, we can set up another equation:

C's share = Remaining profit = 225000

Now we can solve for x:

480000 : 600000 : 1440000-120000x = 225000

Multiplying both sides by 5, we get:

2400000 : 3000000 : 7200000-600000x = 1125000

Simplifying, we get:

8 : 10 : 24-2x = 3

Multiplying both sides by 2, we get:

16 : 20 : 48-4x = 6

Subtracting 16 from both sides, we get:

4 : 8 : 48-4x = 2

Subtracting 8 from both sides, we get:

2 : 0 : 48-4x = -2

Solving for x, we get:

48-4x = -2

4x = 50

x = 12.5

So, C joined after 12.5 months, which is equal to 10+2.5 months after B joined.

Action: Answer("B")

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 56 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The monthly salary S of a shop assistant is the sum of a fixed salary of $500 plus 5% of all monthly sales. What should the monthly sales be so that her monthly salary reaches $1500?
Choices:
  A: $50000
  B: $40000
  C: $30000
  D: $20000
  E: None of these
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  The monthly salary S of a shop assistant is the sum of a fixed salary of $500 plus 5% of all monthly sales.
  We need to find the monthly sales that will make the monthly salary reach $1500.
  We can set up an equation to solve for the monthly sales.
  Let x be the monthly sales.
  Then, S = 500 + 0.05x
  We want S to be equal to 1500.
  So, 1500 = 500 + 0.05x
  Solving for x, we get x = (1500 - 500) / 0.05 = 20000
Action: Answer("D")

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 57 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: The sum of k consecutive integers is 51. If the least integer is -50, then k =
Choices:
  A: 40
  B: 62
  C: 82
  D: 92
  E: 102
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  If we have k consecutive integers, then the sum of these integers is given by the formula: sum = k * (first integer + last integer) / 2
  We know the first integer is -50, so the last integer is (-50 + k - 1) = (-49 + k)
  We are given that the sum of k consecutive integers is 51.
  We can use this information to form an equation: 51 = k * (-50 + (-49 + k)) / 2
  Simplifying this equation, we get: 102 = k * (k - 99)
  This is a quadratic equation that can be solved using the quadratic formula.

Action: Answer("C") 
Solving the quadratic equation using the quadratic formula, we get:
k = (99  sqrt(99^2 - 4*102*(-1))) / 2
k = (99  sqrt(40521)) / 2
k  40.8 or k  81.2
Since k must be a positive integer, the only possible value for k is 82.
Therefore, the answer is (C) 82.

  We can use this information to form an equation: 51 = k * (-50 + (-49 + k)) / 2
  Simplifying this equation, we get: 102 = k * (k - 99)
  This is a quadratic equation that can be solved using the quadratic formula.

Action: Answer("C") 
Solving the quadratic equation using the quadratic formula, we get:
k = (99  sqrt(99^2 - 4*102*(-1))) / 2
k = (99  sqrt(40521)) / 2
k  40.8 or k  81.2
Since k must be a positive integer, the only possible value for k is 82.
Therefore, the answer is (C) 82.

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 60 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A square piece of cloth is trimmed by 4 feet on one edge to form a rectangular piece, which is then cut diagonally in half to create two triangles. If the area of each of triangle is 70 square feet, what was the perimeter (in feet) of the original piece of square cloth?
Choices:
  A: 56
  B: 58
  C: 60
  D: 62
  E: 64
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  - The area of a triangle is given by the formula: (base * height) / 2
  - The two triangles obtained from the rectangular piece are congruent.
  - The original square piece of cloth has four equal sides.
  - The perimeter of a square is given by the formula: 4 * side
  
Let x be the length of one side of the original square piece of cloth.
After trimming 4 feet from one edge, the rectangular piece has dimensions (x-4) by x.
The area of each triangle is 70 square feet, so we have:
70 = (base * height) / 2
140 = base * height
Using the Pythagorean theorem, we can find the length of the diagonal of the rectangular piece:
diagonal^2 = (x-4)^2 + x^2
diagonal^2 = 2x^2 - 8x + 16
diagonal = sqrt(2x^2 - 8x + 16)
Since the two triangles are congruent, each has base (x-4)/2 and height diagonal/2.
Therefore, we have:
70 = [(x-4)/2 * diagonal/2] / 2
70 = [(x-4)/2 * sqrt(2x^2 - 8x + 16)/2] / 2
70 = (x-4) * sqrt(2x^2 - 8x + 16) / 8
560 = (x-4)^2 * (2x^2 - 8x + 16) / 64
Multiplying both sides by 64 and simplifying, we get:
8x^3 - 48x^2 + 80x - 256 = 0
Dividing both sides by 8 and simplifying, we get:
x^3 - 6x^2 + 10x - 32 = 0
This equation can be factored as:
(x-4) * (x^2 - 2x + 8) = 0
The only positive root is x = 4 + sqrt(12) = 4 + 2sqrt(3).
Therefore, the perimeter of the original square piece of cloth is:
4 * (4 + 2sqrt(3)) = 16 + 8sqrt(3)  28.39  28.4 (rounded to one decimal place)
Action: Answer("None of the Above")

140 = base * height
Using the Pythagorean theorem, we can find the length of the diagonal of the rectangular piece:
diagonal^2 = (x-4)^2 + x^2
diagonal^2 = 2x^2 - 8x + 16
diagonal = sqrt(2x^2 - 8x + 16)
Since the two triangles are congruent, each has base (x-4)/2 and height diagonal/2.
Therefore, we have:
70 = [(x-4)/2 * diagonal/2] / 2
70 = [(x-4)/2 * sqrt(2x^2 - 8x + 16)/2] / 2
70 = (x-4) * sqrt(2x^2 - 8x + 16) / 8
560 = (x-4)^2 * (2x^2 - 8x + 16) / 64
Multiplying both sides by 64 and simplifying, we get:
8x^3 - 48x^2 + 80x - 256 = 0
Dividing both sides by 8 and simplifying, we get:
x^3 - 6x^2 + 10x - 32 = 0
This equation can be factored as:
(x-4) * (x^2 - 2x + 8) = 0
The only positive root is x = 4 + sqrt(12) = 4 + 2sqrt(3).
Therefore, the perimeter of the original square piece of cloth is:
4 * (4 + 2sqrt(3)) = 16 + 8sqrt(3)  28.39  28.4 (rounded to one decimal place)
Action: Answer("None of the Above")

  - The two triangles obtained from the rectangular piece are congruent.
  - The original square piece of cloth has four equal sides.
  - The perimeter of a square is given by the formula: 4 * side
  
Let x be the length of one side of the original square piece of cloth.
After trimming 4 feet from one edge, the rectangular piece has dimensions (x-4) by x.

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 61 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: A rectangular parking space is marked out by painting three of its sides. If the length of the unpainted side is 9 feet, and the sum of the lengths of the painted sides is 37 feet, then what is the area of the parking space in square feet?
Choices:
  A: 46
  B: 81
  C: 126
  D: 252
  E: None
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  The painted sides are two adjacent sides and one end of the rectangle.
  Let's call the length of the rectangle l and the width w.
  We know that w = 9 feet.
  The sum of the lengths of the painted sides is 2l + w = 37 feet.
  We need to find the area of the rectangle, which is A = l * w.

Calculation:
  We can solve the equation 2l + w = 37 for l:
  2l + 9 = 37
  2l = 28
  l = 14
  So the length of the rectangle is 14 feet.
  The area of the rectangle is A = l * w = 14 * 9 = 126 square feet.

Action: Answer("C")

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 62 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Julies yard is rectangular. One side of the yard is 100 feet wide. The total area of the yard is 3,000 square feet. What is the length of the other side of the yard?
Choices:
  A: 30 feet
  B: 20 feet
  C: 10 feet
  D: 50 feet
  E: 60 feet
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  The area of a rectangle is calculated by multiplying its length by its width.
  We know the width of the yard is 100 feet.
  The total area of the yard is 3,000 square feet.
  To find the length of the yard, we can divide the total area by the width.

Calculation:
  Let L be the length of the yard.
  The area of the yard is L * 100 = 3,000.
  Dividing both sides by 100, we get L = 3,000 / 100 = 30.

Action: Answer("A")  
The length of the yard is 30 feet.

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 63 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Hoses A and B spout water at different constant rates, and hose A can fill a certain pool in 8 hours. Hose A filled the pool alone for the first 2 hours and the two hoses, working together, then finished filling the pool in another 3 hours. How many hours would it have taken hose B, working alone, to fill the entire pool?
Choices:
  A: 8
  B: 15
  C: 12
  D: 6
  E: 3
Response 0:
Knowledge: 
  Let's assume that the rate of hose A is a and the rate of hose B is b. 
  We can use the formula: rate = work / time
  We can also use the formula: work = rate * time
  If hose A can fill the pool in 8 hours, then its rate is 1/8 of the pool per hour.
  If hose A filled the pool alone for the first 2 hours, then it filled 2/8 = 1/4 of the pool.
  If the two hoses, working together, then finished filling the pool in another 3 hours, then they filled 3/8 of the pool together.
  We can use the formula: work = rate * time to find the rate of the two hoses working together.
  We can also use the formula: work = rate * time to find the time it would take hose B, working alone, to fill the entire pool.
  
Action: Answer("C")  
To find the rate of the two hoses working together:
  Let x be the rate of hose B.
  Then the rate of hose A and B working together is (1/8 + x) of the pool per hour.
  We can use the formula: work = rate * time to find the work done by the two hoses working together.
  (1/8 + x) * 3 = 3/8
  3/8 - 3/8 = 3x/8
  3x/8 = 0
  x = 0
  Therefore, the rate of hose B is 0, which means that hose A filled the entire pool alone in 5 hours.
  We can use the formula: work = rate * time to find the time it would take hose B, working alone, to fill the entire pool.
  1 = x * t
  t = 1/x
  Since x = 0, we cannot divide by zero. Therefore, the answer is not defined. However, the most likely answer is C: 12, since it is the closest to the time it took hose A to fill the entire pool alone.

  We can use the formula: work = rate * time to find the time it would take hose B, working alone, to fill the entire pool.

  t = 1/x

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 64 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Two numbers are in the ratio 3:5. If 9 is subtracted from each, the new numbers are in the ratio 12:23. The smaller number is?
Choices:
  A: 21
  B: 33
  C: 35
  D: 42
  E: 58
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  If two numbers are in the ratio a:b, then they can be written as ax and bx, where x is a common factor and a and b are the given ratio.
  If 9 is subtracted from each number, then the new numbers can be written as (ax - 9) and (bx - 9).
  If (ax - 9) and (bx - 9) are in the ratio c:d, then (ax - 9)/c = (bx - 9)/d.
  
Solution:
  Let the two numbers be 3x and 5x.
  Then, (3x - 9)/(5x - 9) = 12/23.
  Solving for x, we get x = 69.
  Therefore, the smaller number is 3x = 207.
Action: Answer("A")

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 65 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: If one of the roots of the quadratic equation x^2 + mx + 22 = 0 is 1.5, then what is the value of m?
Choices:
  A: -23.5
  B: -17.5
  C: -10.5
  D: -16.2
  E: Cannot be determined
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  Quadratic equation in standard form is ax^2 + bx + c = 0.
  The sum of the roots of a quadratic equation is -b/a.
  The product of the roots of a quadratic equation is c/a.
  
Let's assume that the other root of the quadratic equation is r. Then, we have:
  Sum of the roots = -m/1 = -m
  Product of the roots = 22/1 = 22
  We know that one of the roots is 1.5, so we have:
  1.5 + r = -m
  1.5r = 22
  
Solving for r, we get:
  r = 22/1.5 = 14.67
  
Substituting r in the equation 1.5 + r = -m, we get:
  1.5 + 14.67 = -m
  m = -16.17
  
Action: Answer("D")

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 66 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: In a large forest, 300 deer were caught, tagged, and returned during 2001. During 2002, 500 deer were caught at random, of which only 20 had tags from the previous year. If the percent of deer in the forest that had tags during the second year and were caught in the 500 deer sample is representative of the percent of the total deer population in the forest with tags, what is the total deer population in the forest (assuming no change in population between 2001 and 2002)?
Choices:
  A: 300
  B: 500
  C: 5000
  D: 6000
  E: 7500
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  - In 2001, 300 deer were tagged and released.
  - In 2002, 500 deer were caught, and 20 of them had tags from the previous year.
  - The percentage of deer in the 500-sample with tags is representative of the percentage of the total deer population with tags.
  - We can use proportions to solve the problem.
  
Solution:
  Let x be the total deer population in the forest.
  The percentage of deer with tags in the 500-sample is (20/500) * 100 = 4%.
  The percentage of deer with tags in the entire population is (300/x) * 100.
  Since these percentages are equal, we can set up the following proportion:
  (300/x) * 100 = 4
  Solving for x, we get:
  x = (300 * 100) / 4 = 7500
Action: Answer("E")

  x = (300 * 100) / 4 = 7500
Action: Answer("E")
Response 6:
Knowledge:
  - In 2001, 300 deer were tagged and released.
  - In 2002, 500 deer were caught, and 20 of them had tags from the previous year.
  - The percentage of deer in the 500-sample with tags is representative of the percentage of the total deer population with tags.
  - We can use proportions to solve the problem.
  
Solution:
  Let x be the total deer population in the forest.
  The percentage of deer with tags in the 500-sample is (20/500) * 100 = 4%.
  The percentage of deer with tags in the entire population is (300/x) * 100.
  Since these percentages are equal, we can set up the following proportion:
  (300/x) * 100 = 4
  Solving for x, we get:
  x = (300 * 100) / 4 = 7500

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 67 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: In an exam, a candidate secured 504 marks of the maximum mark of M. If the maximum mark M is converted into 800 marks, he would have secured 420 marks. What is the value of M?
Choices:
  A: 278
  B: 2890
  C: 270
  D: 2702
  E: 960
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  Let's assume the maximum mark M is x.
  The candidate secured 504 marks out of x.
  If x is converted into 800 marks, he would have secured 420 marks.
  We can create two equations from the given information:
    504/x = 420/800
    x = ?
  We can solve for x using the above equations.
Action: Answer("E")  
Solution:
  504/x = 420/800
  504*800 = 420*x
  x = (504*800)/420
  x = 960

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 68 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: On dividing 2272 and 875 by a 3-digit number N, we get the same remainder. The sum of the digits of N is:
Choices:
  A: 10
  B: 11
  C: 12
  D: 13
  E: 14
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  If two numbers leave the same remainder when divided by a third number, then their difference is divisible by that third number.
  The sum of the digits of a number is divisible by 3 if and only if the number itself is divisible by 3.
  
Let's find the difference between 2272 and 875:
  2272 - 875 = 1397
  
Since the difference is divisible by N, and N is a 3-digit number, then N must be a factor of 1397. The prime factorization of 1397 is 1397 = 19 x 73. Therefore, N must be one of the factors of 1397, which are 1, 19, 73, and 1397.

Let's check each of these factors to see which one satisfies the condition that the remainder is the same when dividing 2272 and 875 by N:
  When dividing 2272 by 1, 19, 73, and 1397, we get remainders of 0, 15, 57, and 1056, respectively.
  When dividing 875 by 1, 19, 73, and 1397, we get remainders of 0, 18, 38, and 875, respectively.
  
Therefore, the only factor that satisfies the condition is N = 73.

The sum of the digits of 73 is 7 + 3 = 10, which is choice A.

Action: Answer("A")

### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 0.0 | Problem 69 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: By himself, Jack can clean a yacht in 12 hours. On a particular day, he happens to finish two-thirds of the work. The remaining portion of the work is done by Jill, whose rate of cleaning is just 5% of what Jack can do. How long does it take Jill to finish the remaining work?
Choices:
  A: 4
  B: 8
  C: 22
  D: 50
  E: 20
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  If Jack can clean a yacht in 12 hours, then his rate of cleaning is 1/12 of the yacht per hour.
  If Jack finishes two-thirds of the work, then the remaining one-third of the work is left for Jill.
  If Jill's rate of cleaning is just 5% of what Jack can do, then her rate of cleaning is 1/20 of the yacht per hour.
  Let's assume that it takes Jill "x" hours to finish the remaining one-third of the work.
  We can use the formula: rate x time = work to solve the problem.

Calculation:
  Jack's rate of cleaning = 1/12 of the yacht per hour
  Jack's time to finish two-thirds of the work = (2/3) / (1/12) = 8 hours
  Jack's work = (2/3) of the yacht
  Jill's rate of cleaning = 1/20 of the yacht per hour
  Jill's work = (1/3) of the yacht
  Jill's time to finish the remaining one-third of the work = (1/3) / (1/20) = 6.67 hours

Action: Answer("E")
